Zhang Fakui Resigns from Military Post 40

Willing to Go to the Northeast to Help With the National Crisis as a Citizen

(Hong Kong) Zhang Fakui submitted his resignation because the Guangdong government and the Commander-in-Chief of the Fourth Group Army did not approve of aiding Heilongjiang, and he had the heart to save the country but could not die. The original text is as follows: "Submitted for the purpose of requesting resignation. The Japanese bandits are rampant and invading our country. Liaoning and Jilin have fallen, and Heilongjiang is following. China has raised millions of soldiers, but no one dares to speak of war, sitting and waiting for death, is it not suicide? I am a soldier and should be willing to die. I only know how to save the country and do not care about anything else. Therefore, I have repeatedly asked to go to Heilongjiang to help, but for more than a month, I have not been approved. I heard that the National Government has issued an order to prepare for an expedition, and your seat has spoken of going to the national crisis together. All officers and soldiers of the army are overjoyed, so I rushed back while sick to ask for instructions on the key points. However, things did not go as planned, and the departure was indefinitely delayed. The sincerity of saving the country is foolish, and I cannot die. The people and subordinates of the country are accusing each other. The government may have other difficulties, but the masses cannot forgive it. After thinking again and again, I can only resign from my various positions, so that I can go to the Northeast to help with the national crisis as a citizen, to repay the Party and the country and thank the people. My sincere loyalty, I beg you to examine and approve it, and I also beg you to forward it to the National Government for the record, it is convenient for the public." Presented by Zhang Fakui, former commander of the Fourth Group Army and Commander of the Fourth Army, Military Committee member, Fourth Group Army Frontier Commander. (Eighteenth, Special Dispatch)

International Important Telegrams

Japanese Minseito Party Opposes Government Budget Outline 65

Tokyo Stock Exchange Opens Yesterday

Yoshizawa Plans a Short Stay in Russia

Saionji's Condition Slightly Improves

▲ Domei, Tokyo, 18th - The Minseito Party is paying close attention to the new cabinet's budget plan. Observing the published outline, the financial reorganization largely follows the previous cabinet's plan, but it rejects tax increases and tariff increases, instead using the issuance of public bonds as a source of funds. Yesterday, in the name of Secretary-General Nagai, the following opposition opinion was published: "The new government's budget policy destroys the tax system reorganization created by the previous cabinet to correct the imbalance of the national burden, abandoning the tax increase plan with social policy significance (because the tax increase makes the class with tax-paying ability bear the burden), and its alternative source of funds is sought from public bonds to deal with the temporary. This policy is deceiving the people and destroying the foundation of finance. At the same time as banning the export of gold, it deteriorates international lending and leads the people's lives to danger. Therefore, our party absolutely cannot recognize it."

▲ Rengo, Tokyo, 18th - The Tokyo Stock Exchange decided to open today.

▲ Rengo, New York, 17th - The Japanese exchange rate here fell again today, closing at 40.875, 4.25 lower than yesterday.

Page 10

▲ Kokumin, Moscow, 17th - The newly appointed Japanese Foreign Minister Yoshizawa, on his way back to his new post from France, will stay here for a day or two, to discuss various matters relating to the two countries with Soviet Russian Foreign Affairs Commissioner Litvinov, with particular emphasis on the Manchurian problem. Political circles here are paying close attention to Yoshizawa's actions.

▲ Kokumin, Tokyo, 18th - Saionji, Japan's only surviving elder statesman, entered Kyoto after the dissolution of the Wakatsuki cabinet to present his views to the Emperor, but Saionji is 92 years old and caught a cold on the way. After arriving in Kyoto, he fell ill and the doctor ordered him to rest completely. Today it was reported that Saionji's condition had slightly improved.

Dr. Motta Elected President of Switzerland 66

▲ Kokumin, Bern, 17th - The Swiss Federal Assembly today elected the new President for 1932, Dr. Motta, who will take office on January 1st next year. The doctor is 60 years old and this is his fourth term as president.

Student Riot in Bulgaria 67

Communists Seize the Opportunity to Agitate

Fierce Fighting with Police

▲ Kokumin, Sofia, 17th - A serious student riot occurred at the National University here today. Hundreds of radical students attempted to prevent Prime Minister Mushanov from giving a speech, demanding his resignation. After achieving their goal, they marched to the Parliament to demonstrate. At that time, hundreds of rioters joined the group, including dozens of communists, who are said to have instigated the riot. After the demonstrators arrived at the Parliament, a representative of the Agrarian Party spoke to the crowd from the window, using inflammatory language. The demonstrators became more excited. The police rushed to intervene, causing a fierce battle between the two sides. Several students died and dozens were injured, and the police also suffered some casualties. Due to the public unrest, the authorities announced martial law tonight.

Possible Changes to the Chairman of the International Disarmament Conference 68

Selection of German Delegation Determined

▲ Kokumin, Geneva, 17th - League of Nations Disarmament Committee Director Agethenet will probably persuade former British Prime Minister Henderson to give up his post as Chairman of the Disarmament Conference. He has already gone to Cannes tonight because Henderson is recuperating there. Although officials say that Agethenet's trip is only to consult with Henderson on a few specific issues related to the conference, the public does not believe this, because since Henderson was elected as Chairman of the Conference, there have been new developments that make it inconvenient for Henderson to continue in this role and hinder the progress of the conference. Henderson's attitude is not yet known. Perhaps, due to physical weakness, he will retire voluntarily.

▲ Havas, Berlin, 17th - The German delegation to the Disarmament Conference has been decided by the Central Government. The list has not yet been made public, but according to reliable sources, the delegation will be led by Prime Minister Brüning, with Defense Minister General Gröner and Vice Minister Buhrow accompanying him. Brüning will only attend the opening ceremony in Geneva and participate in the initial general discussions. As for the permanent representative during the Disarmament Conference, Ambassador to Turkey Nadolny will be the chairman.

Scheduled to Convene on January 15th

Advisory Committee Drafting Report

▲ Kokumin, Basel, 17th - According to sources close to the Bank for International Settlements tonight, the report drafted by the Advisory Committee investigating Germany's debt-paying ability will only state the facts and refrain from making judgments, leaving everything to the International Reparations Conference to decide. The conference is scheduled to convene on January 15th in Brussels or London. It is said that the report can be drafted today and submitted to the plenary session of the committee tomorrow. The committee will adjourn no later than Monday of next week in Kyoto.

Gandhi Denies Inflammatory Remarks Reported by Italian Newspaper 70

Authorities in India Strictly Curb Anti-Rent Movement

▲ Reuters, London, 17th - Gandhi replied to a question from a friend in London by radio today, denying the remarks he made to an Italian newspaper in Rome a few days ago, saying that the interview published by the Italian newspaper was completely fabricated. He did not receive a newspaper reporter in Rome, only talked to guests in Villeneuve, Switzerland. At that time, he asked the people of India not to make a decision hastily, but to wait for his report. He will never take hasty action, and even if he has to do so, he will try his best to ask the authorities to allow it.

▲ Reuters, Allahabad, India, 18th - Landlords have cooperated with the authorities to curb the anti-rent movement. According to recent government decrees, local officials are authorized to order landlords to arrest anti-rent propagandists, secretly observe the actions of All India Congress workers, and seize and destroy seditious leaflets.

Britain Restricts Dumping of Foreign Goods 71

Issues Third Tax Increase Order

▲ Reuters, London, 18th - The Ministry of Commerce is now using the privileges granted by the Emergency Import Act to prevent the dumping of foreign goods in Britain. Last night, the Ministry of Commerce issued a third order, announcing today that all goods listed on the list will be subject to a 50% ad valorem tax from tomorrow. The Emergency Import Act allows for a tax of 100%, but in fact, a tax of 50% is enough to prevent the import of foreign goods. The goods subject to this 50% tax are quite numerous, such as glassware, cameras, photographs, radio parts, electric lights, fabrics made of all cotton and half cotton, flags, towels, shawls, tablecloths or bedspreads, face towels, men's and women's socks, and various chemicals.

Austrian Government Orders Political Parties to Ceasefire 72

▲ Reuters, Vienna, 18th - The Austrian government, following the example of the German government, issued an order today requiring political parties to cease fire and prohibiting public gatherings and demonstrations from December 19th to January 1st.

▲ Reuters, London, 18th - The New Transport News today disclosed the details of China using 3 million pounds of British Boxer Indemnity to purchase railway and engineering materials in Britain, saying that 120 40-ton cars and 20 third-class passenger cars have been ordered for the Jinpu Railway, and 40 10-ton cars have been ordered for the Nanjing Construction Committee to reorganize the Anhui coal mines. In addition, there is an order to purchase 10 locomotives.

Important News

22nd Meeting of the National Government Standing Committee 75

▲ Promulgation of Regulations on Handover of Public Servants

▲ Approval of the Abolition of the Headquarters of the Guard Army

The 22nd Standing Committee meeting of the National Government was held on the 18th, attended by Lin Sen, Yu Youren, Yang Shuzhuang, Ding Weifen, Shao Yuanchong, Chen Mingshu, Wang Boqun, Ma Fuxiang, He Yingqin, Wu Tiecheng, and Zhu Peide, with Lin Sen presiding. The following items were discussed: (1) Resolved to promulgate the Regulations on Handover of Public Servants. (2) Resolved to promulgate the amended Articles 13 and 16 of the Implementation Law of the Trade Union Law. (3) Resolved to appoint Xu Wenlong, Liu Enrong, Wu E, and Yue Sun Honglin as prosecutors of the Northeast Branch of the Supreme Court. (4) Resolved to appoint Kan Yuze and Shao Xunyu as division chiefs of the Northeast Branch of the Supreme Court, and Li Dong, Lin Zusheng, Zhou Yunhui, Chen Guangde, Yang Yulin, Wang Zhidong, Wang Chichang, and Zhang Jian as judges of the Northeast Branch of the Supreme Court. (5) Resolved to appoint Wang Jun as the principal of the Infantry School of the Army, Liao Shiqiao as the director of education, and Zhou Bin as the principal of the Artillery School of the Army. (6) Resolved to appoint Zhang Huafu as the infantry supervisor of the Directorate General of Training. (7) Resolved to appoint Liu Ruxian as a senator of the Military Advisory Council. (8) Resolved that Shu Shifu, the military advisor and director of the General Affairs Bureau, has been assigned another position, and is dismissed from his concurrent positions. The vacancy of the director of the General Affairs Bureau will be filled by the military advisor Tian Shijie concurrently. (9) Gu Zhutong, the commander of the Guard Army, reported that according to the organizational law of the provincial government, the chairman and members of the provincial government shall not concurrently hold military positions. As he is now appointed as a member and chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, he should comply with the regulations and resign from his concurrent positions as commander of the Guard Army and commander of the 1st Division to comply with the law. Furthermore, the establishment of the Headquarters of the Guard Army was originally temporary. Now that the Garrison Headquarters of Nanjing and Shanghai has been organized and established, it is proposed to abolish the name of the Headquarters of the Guard Army. Resolved to approve.

Zang Shiyi Willing to be Surrounded by Japanese 76

▲ American Reporter Visiting Zang Denied by Japanese

▲ Li Yi Discusses Zang's Current Environment

The American Evening News, Shenyang, 17th, reports that the correspondent of the American Evening News went to see Zang Shiyi this morning and presented his card to the gatekeeper, asking him to lead him to Zang's office. After waiting for a while, a Japanese man in a suit came out, claiming to be Zang's private secretary, saying that Chairman Zang was very busy and had no time to meet with news reporters. He instructed the reporter (American Evening News) to prepare a number of questions and leave them for reply in a few days. The reporter asked why Japanese newspapers had published news of Zang's interview with news reporters, but he had no time to meet with an American reporter. The Japanese man directly replied that Chairman Zang could not meet with the American reporter at this time. He asked to leave a phone number and be notified later. The reporter then asked if there were any Chinese employees in the office who could lead him to Chairman Zang's office. The Japanese man coldly replied that they were upstairs. Then the reporter walked to the waiting room and waited quietly for development. At that time, a Chinese man, Li Yijun, appeared. Li once served as the magistrate of Shenyang County, saying that Zang was very willing to meet with news reporters, but was obviously inconvenient due to the current environment. He was very sorry. He also said that Zang reluctantly agreed to be the chairman at the request of merchants and businessmen who were dissatisfied with the administration of Yuan Jinkai's maintenance association and requested Zang to be the chairman, hoping to restore order in the province. As for Zang's future attitude towards Zhang Xueliang or the central government, it is not yet possible to say, because the chairman believes that the provincial government is only temporary, so the future political issues of the three northeastern provinces must be decided in the future. The reporter asked if the Japanese newspapers quoted Zang's remarks criticizing Zhang Xueliang and Chiang Kai-shek. Li leaned forward and spoke secretly to the reporter, claiming that he did not believe the reliability of this statement, because Zang and Zhang Xueliang were old friends for many years. The reporter then asked about the Japanese newspaper's statement that Zang would ask the Japanese army to drive out the Chinese troops in Jinzhou. Li said that Zang could not make this request, but the Japanese army might make this statement so that it could use this as an excuse to send troops to Jinzhou. Later, Li secretly told the reporter that Zang was completely surrounded by Japanese secret agents and was not free at all, and was also completely unfamiliar with the local situation in the three northeastern provinces and the political situation in China. He only took the position of chairman because he could not bear to reject the requests of those who own property here. The reporter then asked when the inauguration ceremony would be held. Li replied that it would be within a day or two, but finally Li also admitted that Zang had not seen any local Chinese since he was detained and released by the Japanese, and those who had seen him were only Japanese soldiers. At this point in the conversation, a servant rushed into the room and told Li that the chairman did not want him to talk to the American news reporter. The reporter had no choice but to say goodbye and leave. The American consul here has been trying to meet with Zang, but has not been able to do so, only getting a statement that Zang will issue a declaration soon.

Lu Dipeng Arrives in Hangzhou to Take Over 77

▲ Lu Rui Takes Over the Secretariat of the Provincial Government

The newly appointed Chairman of the Zhejiang Provincial Government, Lu Dipeng, arrived in Hangzhou at 8:40 PM last night (the 17th). Zheng Wenli, the President of the High Court, Zhu Mingtao, the Director of the Security Department, Yu Jishi, the Commander of the Respectful Teacher, Chen Xianghui, the Secretary of the Provincial Government, Wang Ying, the Director of the Finance Department, Zhao Zhiyou, the Mayor of Hangzhou, He Yun, the Director of the Public Security Bureau, and Wang Zhuzhai, the President of the Chamber of Commerce, all arrived at the station earlier to welcome him. As the train approached the platform, the military music played loudly. When the train stopped, Zheng, Wang, and others boarded the train to welcome him. Lu greeted them with a smile. After exchanging pleasantries, he got off the train and walked out of the station, taking the Provincial Government's No. 1 car directly to the Chenglu to rest. At 8:00 AM this morning (the 18th), Lu visited friends at the foot of the South City. At 11:00 AM, accompanied by his nephew, Secretary-General Lu Rui, Secretary Zheng Yanzhuo, and Adjutant Yang Yangyun, and escorted by Section Chief Lu Yuejiang of the Security Department, he arrived at the government. Lu was wearing a navy blue Zhongshan suit and a gray felt hat, looking very tall and dignified, with an amiable attitude. He went to the conference room of the provincial government and met with Zhang Nanxian, arranging to officially take over the government in the afternoon. Then he said goodbye and left. After Zhang saw Lu off, he summoned the staff of the Secretariat, the Security Department, and the Civil Affairs Department to the auditorium to say goodbye. At 2:00 PM, Lu arrived at the government to assume office. The new Secretary-General Lu Rui took over the Secretariat and met with the staff, instructing them to work with peace of mind as usual.

Replacement of Mayor of Qingdao 78

▲Hu Ruoyu transferred to Beiping

▲Shen Honglie temporarily acting as Mayor

Qingdao correspondence: The talk of replacing the Mayor of Qingdao has been circulating for many days. However, due to many difficulties in selecting a successor, it has been delayed. Mayor Hu Ruoyu left Qingdao for Beiping a few days ago, taking his family and luggage with him. It was speculated that he might not return to his post. Indeed, yesterday (the 15th), Zhang Xueliang telegraphed that Hu Ruoyu had been transferred to work in the Beiping Deputy Commander's Office. His vacant post as Mayor of Qingdao has been submitted to the Executive Yuan, and Shen Honglie, Deputy Commander of the Northeast Navy, has been temporarily appointed to act concurrently. After receiving the telegram, Mr. Shen officially took over at the Municipal Government Hall at 4 PM today (the 16th). The details of the replacement and Mr. Shen's assumption of office are described below:

▲Process of Replacing the Mayor: Since the Northeast Incident, there have been rumors of Hu Ruoyu resigning. Zhang Xueliang did send someone to signal to Han Fuju, Chairman of the Shandong Provincial Government, asking him to recommend someone to take over. However, Han, considering the national crisis, felt it was inappropriate to participate in the change of local officials and humbly declined. However, Hu's attitude was passive, and he repeatedly telegraphed Beiping to resign. At the same time, Zhang also faced difficulties with the Northeast Navy's finances. If Mr. Shen concurrently serves as the Mayor of Qingdao, funds for the navy can be raised nearby. Furthermore, since Mr. Shen has been in Qingdao for many years and has connections with people from all walks of life, it would be easier to handle affairs. This is how Hu left and Shen succeeded.

▲Mr. Shen's Assumption of Office: Shen Honglie officially took office at the Municipal Government Hall at 4 PM today. About 400 representatives from all sectors and municipal government officials attended. After taking office, Mr. Shen announced three policy guidelines for the future: (1) Division between the Navy and Municipal Affairs: As a military man concurrently serving as Mayor, the boundaries between military and municipal affairs must be clearly defined because the nature of the Navy and municipal affairs are completely different. The Navy is consumptive and defensive, while municipal affairs are constructive and conservative. Although their natures are opposite, their functions complement each other completely. Since Qingdao was taken over, all administrative affairs have made steady progress. I will follow the established rules and regulations. Regarding municipal construction matters, whether predetermined by the previous administration or not yet planned, as long as they benefit the local area, I will do my best to carry them out and will never let the Navy affect municipal affairs. This is in terms of funding. As for personnel and administration, they will also never be mixed to hinder the progress of municipal affairs. (2) Cultivating Local Vitality: To cultivate local vitality, it is essential to eliminate corruption and promote benefits. The city has a large population with diverse backgrounds, making it difficult to avoid bad habits. Mayor Hu has always been committed to eradicating social ills, and I will continue to do so to cultivate the fundamental morality and physical strength of the citizens. As for promoting benefits, there are many aspects, but the most important are education and port affairs. Since Mayor Hu took office, port affairs have made significant progress. For example, the Port Affairs Fund Custody Committee is well-intentioned and beautifully managed, and I will continue to do so as before. Education should be practical, and this aspect will be discussed with the competent authorities to make contributions. (3) Maintaining Local Tranquility: Maintaining public order in this city, where Chinese and foreigners live together, is the most important responsibility of the military and government authorities. This should be divided into symptomatic and fundamental treatments. For the past ten years, the Navy has cooperated with the Public Security Bureau to maintain public order in the city. Fortunately, there have been no major incidents. In the future, the military and police should strengthen their joint defense. However, this is a symptomatic treatment. The fundamental solution lies in the citizens' clear understanding of the country's status and the city's status, as well as the responsibilities of citizens, with a spirit of unity, and using self-governance to govern others to the best of their abilities. On the one hand, it prevents the hiding of local scoundrels, and on the other hand, it integrates with local foreigners. If everyone can be self-reliant and there is a sound society, there will be no hidden worries. After Mr. Shen's speech, City Party Department representative Yi Yiwun, Councillor Miu Mengxiong, and City Chamber of Commerce Chairman Song Yuting spoke in succession, followed by a group photo and dismissal. (December 16)

Local Correspondence

Suzhou 81

Continuation of Middle School Students Destroying the Party Headquarters: The incident of students from various middle schools in Wuxian destroying the Party Headquarters and beating Party Committee members was reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now learned that the Party Committee members also reported the injuries and destruction to the Provincial Party Headquarters that night, requesting instructions. Some committee members went to the province on the 18th to report in person. Yesterday (the 18th) at 9 AM, about 1,000 students from various schools arrived at the sports field. At 10:30 AM, they went to the County Party Headquarters, but there were only a few service staff inside and no Party Committee members were seen. However, they saw that the portrait of Sun Yat-sen and the national flag in the auditorium had been destroyed by the Party Headquarters themselves. Therefore, they turned to the County Government to petition. The County Magistrate was out on official business, so Zhao Jintang came out to meet the students. The students demanded three points: (1) Guarantee patriotic movements. (2) The Public Security Bureau must not suppress patriotic movements. (3) Demand proof that the portrait of Sun Yat-sen and the national flag in the County Party Headquarters were torn down by the Party Headquarters themselves, and that the Party Headquarters should apologize to the students. Mr. Zhao agreed to convey this to the County Magistrate, and the students dispersed.

Changshu 82

Middle School Students in the County Suspend Classes: Yesterday, the County Middle School received an instruction from the Jiangsu Provincial Student Union, stating that from the 17th, all classes should be suspended to carry out propaganda. The County Middle School, upon receiving the order, immediately requested Principal Xu Yunfu to announce the suspension of classes. The Principal was unable to stop them, but for the sake of curriculum, initially only agreed to suspend classes for three days. The students refused, and finally announced a two-week suspension of classes to carry out propaganda in various places.

Former Construction Bureau Director Moved to the Police Station for Supervision: Former Director of the County Construction Bureau, Chen Qiwei, was detained by the new Director, Wang Yizeng, who telegraphed the province due to numerous improprieties in the handover procedures. The Public Security Bureau was requested to send personnel to guard Chen's residence, which has been going on for a month. However, the local Public Security Bureau found it extremely troublesome to rotate officers on duty every day. Therefore, Director Yin negotiated with Chen, asking if Chen could temporarily reside in the Bureau to avoid complications, to which Chen agreed. He was moved to the Bureau the day before yesterday. On the 17th, the Construction Department sent technician Lu Yizhi to Changshu to investigate the case. It is heard that there are three important points: (1) The Changtai Highway project is unfinished, and the expenses have exceeded the original amount. Are there any inflated expenditures? (2) Problems with the relocation of graves and cattle sheds. (3) Are there any errors in the earthwork of the Changtai Road and the tea and water expenses issued? It is heard that Lu has gained some insight and will soon leave Changshu.

Wuxi 83

Improvement of Party Affairs Organization and Federation of Labor Unions: Since the establishment of the Executive and Supervisory Committee in Wuxi, the isolation between the Party Headquarters and the Party members has led to the dissipation of the will of Party members throughout the county. In particular, committee members from other regions have behaved improperly and were criticized by the general public and left. Recognizing the current situation, comrades in the county believe that Party affairs must be improved. Yao Xinchui was elected chairman and the following important matters were resolved: (1) Organize a Wuxi County Party Affairs Improvement Committee. (2) The number of committee members is set at 15. (3) Appoint Yao Xinchui, Xu Chizi, Hu Tongsheng, Wang Zhiming, Zhu Zuyin, Ni Tieru, Jiang Bo

Yu Ru, Hua Ti, etc. as improvement committee members. (4) Issue a letter to the public in the name of the joint meeting of the Executive and Supervisory Committee members of various districts. (5) Immediately notify the County Executive and Supervisory Committee to handle the handover in the name of the joint meeting. After the meeting, the first committee meeting was held, and it was resolved to appoint Xu Chizi, Zhu Zuyin, Yao Xinchui, Mao Junbai, and Wang Zhiming as standing committee members. Hu Tongsheng was appointed Director of the General Affairs Section, Yang Yuru was appointed Director of the Propaganda Section, Qian Heqing was appointed Director of the Organization Section, and Hu Bin was appointed Director of the Training Section. Wang Zhiming, Mao Junbai, and Yao Xinchui were appointed as committee members responsible for drafting the declaration of the committee, and the standing committee members were responsible for receiving the County Executive and Supervisory Committee. After being commissioned, Xu and Tang came to Wuxi the day before yesterday and convened a joint meeting of labor unions yesterday. Representatives from 27 silk and yarn industries attended. The meeting ended, and it was heard that a mass meeting of labor unions throughout the county would be convened in the near future.

Anti-Japanese Work During the Suspension of Classes: All middle and higher schools in Wuxi have expressed serious concerns about the current situation and have unanimously endured the pain of suspending classes. Yesterday, the seventh representative conference was held, and four goals for the suspension of classes were decided: (1) Request Chairman Lin to announce the national salvation policy and punish Foreign Minister Gu Weijun. (2) Request the National Government to order Zhang Xueliang to recover the lost territory within a time limit. (3) Request the Guangdong Central Committee members to go to Beijing immediately to organize a unified government and implement revolutionary diplomacy. (4) Explicitly guarantee the patriotic movement. It is heard that the above four points have been sent by express mail to the Nanjing Central Party Headquarters, the National Government's Acting Chairman Lin, and the Guangdong Central Committee members for reply.

Store Closures: This year, the spring, summer, and autumn seasons in the county have been disappointing. The crops have been submerged, and the violent sun has occupied our Eastern Provinces. The national crisis is not over, and the market has plummeted. Financial panic has reached its peak. Taichang Cotton Seed Shop, which drifts sesame cakes outside the North Gate along the river, will close due to financial difficulties. The total loss is more than 20,000 yuan. Three money shops owe more than 9,000 yuan to the shop without any compensation. In addition, Zhou Yichang Coal Company in Beitang Coal Yard has also been stranded due to poor turnover, with a huge loss. As the weather is cold and the year is coming to an end, it is feared that there will be a succession of merchants who cannot maintain their business.

The prisoners elected Chi Fufu as their representative and demanded four points: (1) The meal should still be twenty taels. (2) The original rice bowls are broken and need to be replaced. (3) Restore bathing once a week. (4) Shi Zaiqing should be released (Shi was previously punished for arguing over food). Hua expressed acceptance of three points and the fourth point would be handled after investigation. The prisoners agreed to resume eating, and the matter was resolved. Coastal Harbors Along the Yangtze River are Closed: Due to the recent unrest among coastal bandits along the Yangtze River in Nantong, Rugao, Haimen, Qidong, and other counties, it has been agreed that all remote small harbors will be closed by the water police to prevent bandits from smuggling weapons. As the private Zhenjiang Middle School had not attended the scene, students from the school reported that it was because the principal did not allow them to join. Thousands of male and female students present were greatly agitated and rushed to the school, taking Principal Shen Pingzhou to the Memorial Tower at Dashikou and questioning him about his reasons for not participating. Shen's words were ambiguous, so the students wrote "Shen Pingzhou who obstructs students' patriotic movement" on a piece of paper, pasted it on his back, and forced him to parade with them. Mr. Hu was quite embarrassed and unable to respond. Chairman Ye promised to find a way, and the staff retreated.

Yangzhou 87

Twists and Turns in Repairing the Canal Dike: It has been four months since the breach of the canal. Although the provincial government has made many plans, and the people of Jiangbei have repeatedly appealed, the project is too large and a complete calculation shows that it cannot be completed without four million yuan. Chairman Ye and Director Shen of the Construction Department convened representatives from Huaiyang counties to the province and announced to the public that there was already one million yuan from the province and one million yuan from the central government. The shortfall would be covered by 50,000 tons of American wheat, which could be used for work-for-relief purposes. It was said that the hope of the people of Jiangbei for the early restoration of the canal dike could absolutely be realized. Unexpectedly, the Jiangsu Provincial Government was reorganized, and it was recently learned from Beijing that the one million yuan assisted by the National Government had not been secured. The result of the provincial treasury's one million yuan was that the Finance Department only had 600,000 yuan and the amount of American wheat could not be determined. When the news came, the executive committee members of the Water Disaster Relief Association and the Water Disaster Tragedy Relief Association were extremely panicked. If the Beijing news is not false, the canal dike will never be repaired, and the disaster victims in more than ten counties will never have a home to return to. It is heard that the two associations plan to convene a temporary emergency executive committee immediately to discuss countermeasures to avoid delays and make it difficult to start construction. However, Han Zishi, the executive chairman of the association, has gone to Zhenjiang to discuss solutions with the new and old provincial chairmen. The outcome is not yet known.

Gaoyou 88

Large-Scale Salary Demands by All Teachers and Staff: Although various schools and social education institutions in the county have been maintained as usual due to the lack of education funding this year, all teachers and staff, since this year's funding has not been secured and the salary arrears of five and a half months from last year are unlikely to be paid, discussed salary demands at Shixiao School at 3 PM yesterday (14th) and resolved to go to the County Government collectively to demand salaries. When they arrived at the County Government, Section Chief Wang Tingfan of the Third Section received them. At 5 PM this afternoon, everyone gathered at the County Women's Elementary School, and the principals of various schools and the directors of various social education institutions went to the County Government to hear the news.

Education News

Special Article: The Three Principles of the People and University Education (Continued 1) Zheng Hongnian 90

Freedom and equality are also for the liberation of mankind and the pursuit of freedom and equality for all nations. Under today's economic crisis in various countries, the Three Principles of the People can open a path, and there is no need to imitate its aggressive tactics.

3. Goals of University Education

(A) Understanding Modern Culture: The implementation of the Three Principles of the People must be constructed with substantial education. The teaching of Party ideology in schools at all levels can be deep or shallow, but in universities, students should have a thorough understanding. The true value of the Three Principles of the People must be clearly identified. It is difficult to glimpse the foundation of the Three Principles of the People and the reasons for its formation without exploring it from modern culture, and it is not enough to estimate the value of the Three Principles of the People without a world cultural perspective. Today's university education, its curriculum reform and allocation, is a matter for experts. In short, university education that is based on the Three Principles of the People must cultivate talents who understand modern culture and integrate them, so that their thoughts and actions are concentrated on the position of the Three Principles of the People. For the basic social sciences and natural sciences required for national construction, social construction, and material construction, we should study the essence of the theory and focus on the knowledge and skills of production technology in order to create the cultural value of the Three Principles of the People and complete material construction, and cultivate the spirit of hard work and the ability to lead the masses.

(B) Tempering of the Three Principles of the People: The education of the Three Principles of the People cannot be effective simply by promoting the name of the Three Principles of the People, nor can it be accomplished in universities simply by adding a course in Party ideology. All environmental facilities and the entire physical and mental aspects of students must be consistently instilled with the spirit of education of the Three Principles of the People. All sciences should radiate with the Three Principles of the People as the center, and conclude with the function of the Three Principles of the People being present everywhere. Only then can we achieve the independence of the national spirit, the universality of the implementation of civil rights, and the purpose of promoting the people's livelihood. As for the purpose and implementation guidelines of education in the Republic of China, they have been clearly defined by the Third National Congress of the Kuomintang of China, and their detailed planning for implementation has also been carefully reviewed by the Central Executive Committee. The objectives of higher education are excerpted as follows:

1. Students should truly understand the true meaning of the Three Principles of the People and have practical scientific knowledge and skills so as to realize the mission of the Three Principles of the People.

2. Schools should give full play to the functions of academic institutions so as to become cultural centers.

3. The curriculum should be based on the needs of national construction so as to achieve the effect of storing materials for the country.

4. Training should be centered on the Three Principles of the People to cultivate a personality with comprehensive moral, intellectual, physical, aesthetic, and group qualities.

5. Equipment should be as complete as possible and related to curriculum training. According to the above objectives, how should the principles of university education be implemented and equipped to temper talents of the Three Principles of the People? The principles stipulated by the central government can be used as a guideline.

One Kind of Contradictory Phenomenon in the Voice of National Salvation (Continued from yesterday) Hai Factory 91

Some people say that wearing Western suits is a requirement of the times and can make foreigners aware of our cultural progress and look up to us. Is this true? Li Hongzhang-style diplomats, dragging their queues to foreign countries, versus the current diplomats in beautiful Western suits, which ones are really respected by foreigners? Perhaps this is a difference of eras, and there's no need to discuss it. Let's look at the recent example of Gandhi. He goes to England, a country that values the "gentlemanly" spirit and etiquette the most, with only a loincloth and a shawl of homespun cloth, yet he can stand on equal footing and interact with people in grand attire in the resplendent conference room of St. James's Palace. From the King to the common people, everyone respects him very much. I ask, have Chinese diplomats in Western suits ever received such respect from England? India is a conquered nation, having lost all freedom. Gandhi wants to restore India, and he does so simply by wearing homespun cloth and not using British goods. This method has left the British at a loss. China is not yet a conquered nation, and it is so easy to implement the use of domestic goods. I dare say that what Japan and all imperialists fear is Gandhi-style boycott, not slogans and posters. I think that if the Kuomintang did not just shout empty slogans of "Down with Imperialism" but instead strictly ordered all party members and officials at all levels to wear domestic goods, it would be enough to make the imperialists take notice. The oppression and aggression of imperialists against our country are increasing day by day, and the number of Chinese people wearing Western suits is also increasing day by day, especially after the establishment of the Nanjing government, which is directly proportional. This time, when the Japanese invaded Shenyang, they specially abused and killed Chinese people wearing Western suits. Some people were lucky enough to escape by disguising themselves as farmers. From this, can it be said that wearing Western suits can really make foreigners look up to us?

I am not like a stubborn old gentleman, absolutely advocating the preservation of long gowns and mandarin jackets, saying that Western suits are the clothing of barbarians. If China could supply all the materials for Western suits in the future, I would also very much support everyone wearing Western suits, but we can't talk about that now. What material used for Western suits now is not from abroad? The Japanese widely began to wear Western suits only after their country could manufacture the materials for them, which is different from the backbone of the Chinese. In this world, only those who truly love their country can be respected by foreigners. Gandhi is a good example. People who say they love their country but use foreign goods all over their bodies are not truly patriotic. Only those who are looked down upon by foreigners have anything beautiful to say, or have any chance to show off? Foreign goods in China have already permeated everywhere like mercury. Besides clothing materials, there are certainly many foreign goods that Chinese people do not need to use but insist on using. However, clothing is essential to life and has the greatest consumption, so we must pay attention to it first. Male and female students, do you want to save the country? Please do not use foreign-made clothing. Teachers, do you want to save the country? Please do not wear foreign-made clothing for students to see. This is something that patriotic comrades must do and is the easiest thing to do. If this small expression of genuine patriotism cannot be done, is not willing to be done, or is not willing to be done thoroughly, then please do not put up posters, do not shout slogans, do not strike and demonstrate, do not send telegrams, do not go to Beijing to petition. Everyone should just wait sloppily to become slaves of a conquered nation. (To be continued)

Chen Hexian, Director of the Jiangsu Department of Education, Has Handed Over His Duties 93

The Jiangsu Provincial Government has been reorganized, and Director Chen of the Department of Education immediately ordered all departments to rush to hand over their duties. Yesterday, the handover was completed clearly. All payment orders from the provincial treasury, totaling more than 76,000 yuan, and various special education funds and relief funds, totaling about 10,000 yuan in cash, were all registered in full, awaiting the new appointee to take over. In addition, the remaining amount of donations for the construction of the Central Party Headquarters, totaling more than 4,000 yuan, was also submitted to the provincial government for verification and forwarding. Director Chen managed to raise enough money on his own to pay the salaries of the department's staff until the day he handed over his duties. It is said that Director Chen left the province that night.

Students From Various Universities Return to Shanghai Completely at One O'Clock This Morning After Demonstrating in Beijing 95

▲ A total of more than 2,200 students arrived

▲ No general demonstration held in Beijing

▲ Wensheng holds a meeting to mourn the dead

More than 6,000 students from various universities in this city organized a demonstration delegation to Beijing. After arriving in Beijing successively on the 14th and 15th, they originally planned to join students from Beijing, Tianjin, and other places to hold a general demonstration yesterday and a large parade on the 17th. However, since the 17th, when a part of the students clashed with the military police, the demonstration delegations from Tianjin and other places were urged by the army to return to their original places of origin yesterday. The Shanghai demonstration delegation to Beijing took a special train from Beijing Railway Station to Shanghai at 4:00 p.m. yesterday and arrived in port completely at 1:00 a.m. this morning. The details are recorded separately below.

▲ Military Police Guard: According to a reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency, after the demonstration delegations from various places clashed with the military police in Beijing the day before yesterday, the Beijing Garrison Command immediately alerted the Central University. The schools were where the demonstration delegations from various places resided. At that time, a small number of personnel from the Tianjin demonstration delegation were forced to return to Tianjin. By yesterday morning, the security was even stricter, and the military police went to the Central University to persuade the students to return immediately. At that time, the students from Jinan were escorted back to Jinan. Students from Anhui, Suzhou, and other places also returned to their hometowns one after another. The students from Shanghai were able to leave only at 4:00 p.m. A special train was dispatched from the railway station, and the army sent them to the station and ordered them to board the train immediately. The general demonstration that students from various places had planned to hold in Beijing yesterday was thus disbanded.

▲ Number of Returnees: The number of returnees is estimated as follows: 300 from Tongji, more than 30 from Tongji Supervisor College, 100 from the Medical School of Central University, more than 10 from the Business School of Central University, more than 100 from Chizhi, more than 50 from Guanghua, 200 from Fudan and its affiliated middle school, more than 50 from Jinan, more than 30 from Wenhua, more than 60 from Southeast Medical School, more than 200 from Dongya, more than 50 from Jiangnan, 20 from Liangjiang, 20 from Wensheng, 50 from Law School, more than 100 from Jiaotong University, and hundreds from the French Institute of Technology, the Central Public School, Shanghai Middle School, and Pudong Middle School, totaling about 2,200 to 2,300 people.

▲ Mourning the Dead: Yang Tongheng (erroneously written as Yang Tongheng), courtesy name Xintian, a student from Wensheng Higher English School who was killed in Beijing this time, was from Xuanzhang County, Sichuan. He graduated from the county middle school and worked as a teacher at a primary school in Daxian County. He wanted to specialize in English, so he came to Shanghai and entered the third year of Wensheng. His family is currently in Sichuan and has not yet been informed. Yesterday, the school held an emergency meeting to discuss the matter. Because Yang was very diligent at school, a memorial service will be held to mourn the deceased.

▲ Xiamen University Arrives in Shanghai: Xiamen University also organized a delegation to Beijing to petition the government. They arrived in Shanghai on the 16th on the Gongping ship to go to Beijing. It is now possible to reach Shanghai. However, since the capital has suffered this change, the students from the university are afraid that they will not go to Nanjing after arriving in Shanghai and will return to Xiamen immediately. (Xin Sheng News Agency)

Another report: More than 1,800 middle and high school students in this city have left Beijing in batches yesterday to return to Shanghai. The first batch to leave Beijing was more than 300 students from Jinan and Chizhi, who took the 8th express train back to Shanghai yesterday morning and arrived in port at 4:50 p.m. A part of Jinan got off at Zhenru. The second batch, totaling more than 1,500 students, took a special train chartered by the Railway Bureau at 4:15 p.m. yesterday from Nanjing Station and arrived at the North Station at 1:00 a.m. this morning. They were then taken back to school by truck. Students from various schools in Shanghai went to the station to welcome them.

Local News

Jiangsu Elders' Proposals Regarding the Issuance of Public Bonds 105

▲ Pay Attention to Three Points

Jiangsu elders Ma Liang and others issued a joint letter stating: To the national financial community and the people of the entire country: The Nationalist Party has ruled the country with party governance for five years. The impact and extent of its policies on morality and culture are universally seen and heard, and there is no room for concealment. Regarding national finance alone, apart from land taxes, customs duties, salt surplus taxes, unified taxes, and all kinds of harsh and miscellaneous taxes extracted to the utmost, the public bonds issued during these five years, excluding those already repaid, amount to more than 1.1 billion yuan in principal and interest. The use of this huge amount of public bonds has not only failed to contribute to any national construction, but has also failed to benefit tens of millions of disaster victims. Instead, it has been used to instigate civil wars, devastate lives, support dictatorship, eliminate dissidents, suppress public opinion, and deprive freedom, leading to a situation where people are brave in internal struggles but cowardly in public defense. The vast territory of China is shrinking by the day, and the country is in imminent danger, with the people suffering terribly. Alas, who is responsible for this, and how did it come to this? If not for the economic support, how could the country be driven to the brink of ruin? This is something that our national financial community and all compatriots should deeply reflect upon after suffering pain. Each time public bonds are issued, the financial community, intimidated by oppressive power, acts as an agent for sale, which is understandable. However, they are greedy for immediate gains and fail to investigate the purpose of the bonds, recklessly absorbing them without imposing restrictions. The facts are clear, and there is no denying it. As for the Chinese people who subscribe to public bonds, they are preoccupied with profit and neglect everything else. Due to the lack of transparency in financial matters, the amount of bonds is never questioned, until financial stagnation and panic in all industries awakens them, which is also pitiable. It is found that most of these 1.1 billion yuan in public bonds are issued in the corner of Shanghai, and the vast majority are scattered among the people of Jiangsu province. This is the capital earned with the sweat and blood of the people, and it is vital to the nation's lifeline. If public and private finances collapse, and the overall situation is shaken, the consequences would be unimaginable. We are concerned with protecting the rights of public bond holders, rescuing the national economy as a whole, learning from past mistakes, and thinking anxiously. Faced with foreign aggression and the reorganization of the political situation, we dare to offer our sincere request to the national financial community and the people of the entire country to pay attention to three things: (1) After this government reorganization, no matter who forms the new government, it must quickly establish a formal people's political participation mechanism, implement a budget and final account system, and ensure financial transparency. Even if new public bonds are issued within the budget scope, the reasons, quantities, and uses for the issuance must be clearly explained. Otherwise, our financial community and the people of the entire country vow not to subscribe. (2) After this government reorganization, no matter who forms the new government, it must formally recognize all public bonds issued by the previous government, with principal and interest handled according to the original terms. Before the old public bonds are formally recognized by the new government, refuse to sell any new public bonds under any name. (3) From now on, our national financial community and the people of the entire country should not only pay attention to supervising the issuance of domestic public bonds, but also expose and formally reject any attempts by foreign powers to issue large-scale international public bonds under false pretenses, sacrificing national sovereignty, to cut off the source of the government's sins. Do not repeat the previous mistakes of indifference and tolerance. The way to save ourselves and the country lies in this. Our national financial community and the people of the entire country, having experienced such deep pain, must fundamentally change our approach, implement supervision of government powers, so that politics can quickly get on track, end the various disputes of the past twenty years, and create a new life for the Republic of China. Survival is at stake at this critical juncture. We respectfully present our humble opinion, hoping for your public consideration. Ma Liang, Zhao Fengchang, Shen Enfu, Zhang Yijun, Xun Kang, Li Genyuan, Huang Yanpei, Mu Xiangyue, Zhu Shaowen, Leng, Jia Fengzhen, Zhao Ping, Yuan Xiluo, Lu Guiliang, et al., of the Jiangsu Provincial National Crisis Relief Association, respectfully bow.

Dispute Occurred at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce Yesterday 106

▲ The Merchants' Movement Committee Sent Personnel to Take Over

▲ Chamber of Commerce Chairman Wang Xiaolai Refused to Hand Over

▲ 160 Trade Associations Issued a Declaration

New Voice News reports: The Shanghai Special Municipality Merchants' Movement Committee dispatched a large number of personnel to take over the Municipal Chamber of Commerce at Tianhougong Bridge yesterday afternoon, creating a rather serious situation. The Municipal Public Security Bureau and the Municipal Defense Corps were ordered to send police to protect the site. Chairman Wang Xiaolai of the Chamber of Commerce replied that the Chamber of Commerce is a legal organization and cannot be handed over without legal grounds, resulting in the failure of the takeover. At the same time, 160 trade associations in the city also expressed their opposition. The details are as follows:

Situation at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce 107

▲ Disturbance: After 12 noon yesterday, Zhang Zilian led dozens of people who sneaked into the Municipal Chamber of Commerce. They were dressed sloppily, in plain clothes and short outfits, looking quite disreputable. They all carried a symbol on them, a card with the red seal of the Shanghai Special Municipality Merchants' Movement Committee and a number for identification. After the crowd arrived at the Chamber of Commerce, they went to various offices, creating disturbances and intending to cause trouble. Seeing these plainclothes people inside, the Chamber of Commerce realized that their presence would affect the operations, so they separately reported to the Municipal Government, the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, and the Municipal Public Security Bureau, requesting protection. Around 1 pm, police officers from the Public Security Bureau and members of the Defense Corps arrived one after another and drove the plainclothes people out of the Chamber of Commerce, so that the Chamber of Commerce members could resume their normal work.

▲ Authorities Prevented Takeover: After receiving the report, Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, sent officials Chen Zeyi and Hu Yuqi to investigate and report to the Municipal Government. He also notified Wang Xiaolai, Chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, that he was not allowed to hand over the Chamber of Commerce.

▲ Corps and Police Protection: After the Municipal Chamber of Commerce reported to the Municipal Government and requested protection, Acting Mayor Secretary-General Yu Hongjun immediately ordered the Public Security Bureau to send police to protect the site. Acting Director Wang Yuwen ordered Lu Ying, Captain of the Detective Team, together with Sun Mou, Captain of the Sixth Squad of the Police Brigade, and 36 armed police officers, to go to protect the site. The Municipal Defense Corps was also ordered to dispatch the First Defense Post of the Eighth Team stationed in Tanziwan, led by platoon leader Li Shouhai and 40 armed members, to protect the site.

▲ Chairman's Statement: Wang Xiaolai, Chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, arrived at the Chamber of Commerce at 2 pm and learned of the situation. At that time, Zhao Nangong from the Organizing Department of the so-called Merchants' Movement Committee was also at the Chamber of Commerce. The chairman met with them, and Zhao handed over the official letter from the Merchants' Movement Committee to send personnel to take over. Wang Xiaolai immediately stated sternly that the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce was established in accordance with the Chamber of Commerce Law. This Chamber of Commerce Law was passed by Mr. Hu Zhantang when he was the speaker of the Legislative Yuan and was formally promulgated by the National Government. He was elected as the chairman and was legally elected. Only by following the law can the handover be carried out. What is called legal handover is that after the term of office expires, a general meeting of members is convened to re-elect in accordance with the regulations, or the competent authority provides guidance. To go a step further, if the members ask the committee to resign before the term of office expires, there must be sufficient reasons and procedures stipulated by the Chamber of Commerce Law. Otherwise, he can also ask the court to legally protect his position. Therefore, he naturally cannot accept this request. If force is used to coerce him, he will not be afraid. However, the government has the responsibility to maintain law and order, and he will report to the authorities for handling. Moreover, he has no knowledge of who commissioned the so-called Shanghai Special Municipality Merchants' Movement Committee, so how can he rashly hand over the Chamber of Commerce? Now that Beijing and Guangdong are united, all issues will be collectively resolved by the Fourth Central Committee. He is deeply puzzled by the sudden occurrence of this dispute. Zhao left angrily when Wang refused to hand over the Chamber of Commerce.

▲ Standing Committee Members' Remarks: Ye Huijun, Wang Yansong, Xu Jiqi, and Yuan Ludeng, members of the Standing Committee of the Chamber of Commerce, issued a joint statement yesterday, saying that the Municipal Chamber of Commerce is a legal organization organized in accordance with the law, and they were elected as members of the Standing Committee in accordance with the law, so they cannot relinquish their positions unless it is in accordance with the law. This is a very clear principle. Important cases of the Chamber of Commerce must be resolved by the Executive and Supervisory Committee, and its foundation lies in the various trade associations. Their advancement or retreat follows the laws and regulations on the one hand and obeys public opinion on the other. As long as they are in office, they will do their duty and will not be afraid.

▲ Telegraph to the Municipal Government: The Municipal Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Municipal Government and the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau yesterday, stating: To the Shanghai Municipal Government and the Social Affairs Bureau: At about 12 noon today, dozens of plainclothes people suddenly came to the Chamber of Commerce, claiming to take over, with a threatening posture, obstructing the work of the Chamber of Commerce. The Chamber of Commerce was established on June 22, 1929, in accordance with the Chamber of Commerce Law promulgated by the National Government. The current Executive and Supervisory Committee were also legally elected by the general meeting of members on that day and reported to the competent authorities. Now, some plainclothes people are falsely claiming a name and attempting to seize the Chamber of Commerce by force, which not only violates national laws and regulations, but also affects social order. If this is not thoroughly investigated, how can laws and regulations be maintained and organizations be respected? Therefore, we specially report the situation in a telegram, respectfully requesting your government and bureau to investigate and stop it, and order the Municipal Public Security Bureau to send police to maintain order, so that we can work smoothly. We are looking forward to it. Respectfully, the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce.

▲ Important Announcement: The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce issued an important announcement yesterday, stating: Our Chamber of Commerce was formally established on June 22, 1929, in accordance with the Chamber of Commerce Law promulgated by the National Government. The current Executive and Supervisory Committee members are entrusted with the responsibility of managing the affairs of the Chamber of Commerce by all members, and we respect the law. Except for holding re-elections after the term of office of the committee members expires in accordance with the law or following the guidance of the competent authorities, we will not accept any interference in the actions of our Chamber of Commerce from any other individual or organization under any name. Even if force is used to coerce us, we will resolutely reject it. This is a special declaration, hoping that all trade associations in the city and the merchants in the city will take note.

▲ Convene a Meeting: The Chamber of Commerce convened an emergency meeting of the Standing Committee at 5 pm yesterday. Wang Xiaolai, Wang Yansong, Xu Jiqi, Yuan Ludeng, and others attended. The meeting was chaired by Wang Xiaolai. First, the chairman reported on the various situations of the day, and then a unanimous resolution was made to convene an emergency joint meeting of the Executive Committee and the Supervisory Committee to discuss the countermeasures.

▲ Normal Work: After the Municipal Public Security Bureau sent police to the Chamber of Commerce to maintain order and completely drove out the plainclothes team, all departments resumed work immediately, everything returned to normal, and all order was restored.

▲ Yu Qiaqing's Remarks: Yu Qiaqing of the Shipping Association made remarks on this matter yesterday, saying that the Chamber of Commerce is a legal organization of merchants. Its real basic members are the various trade associations. The affairs of the Chamber of Commerce should be resolved by a majority vote of the representatives of various industries. All merchants should unite in unity within the scope of the law. This unfortunate incident in the Chamber of Commerce is considered a violation of the law by a very small number of people, destroying the entire merchant community, which is very painful and should be absolutely stopped. We hope that all legitimate merchants in the city will recognize this.

▲ Situation on the Side of the Merchants' Movement Committee

▲ Committee Established: The Shanghai Special Municipality Merchants' Movement Committee, after being ordered to organize, officially started work yesterday. A special office was set up at No. 384 Jiujiang Road, and a notice was issued stating: Our committee has been ordered to organize and has been established. All matters concerning the merchants' movement in this city will be handled by our committee. We hope that all merchants in the city will take note of this. The standing committee members are Feng Shaoshan, Shi Zhikun, Wang Hanliang, and others. The secretary is Chen Zhiying.

▲ Take Over the Chamber of Commerce: After the Merchants' Movement Committee officially started work, it was resolved to send Zhao Nangong, Director of the Organization Department, Liu Musu, Director of the Special Affairs Department, and Chen Zhiying, the secretary, to Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce to take over, and Zhang Zi led the plainclothes team, each with a symbol, to handle the matter.

▲ Letter to the Chamber of Commerce: The Merchants' Movement Committee sent personnel to take over the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, holding an official letter stating: Dear Sir, The Shanghai Special Municipality General Chamber of Commerce was disrupted and forcibly occupied by the Shanghai Municipal Party Department in April 1929, and then illegally reorganized by the Nanjing Central Party Department, destroying the merchants' movement and violating the true spirit of democratic politics. For three years, the will of the merchants in the city has not been able to express itself, and the suffering is beyond words. Our committee is a group to promote the merchants' movement. Except for the letter, we hereby inform you that you should handle it in accordance with the investigation and immediately hand over the seals, documents, and other items to the aforementioned personnel for clear receipt. This is very important. To the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Shanghai Special Municipality Merchants' Movement Committee.

▲ Takeover Failed: After 12 noon, Zhang Zilian led the team to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce first, and then Chen Zhiying, Liu Musu, Sun Choucheng, and others went to notify the staff of the Chamber of Commerce, explaining the reasons for the takeover, and instructed them to work with peace of mind. Later, Standing Committee Member Wang Hanliang and Organization Director Zhao Nangong also arrived and met with Chairman Wang Xiaolai of the Chamber of Commerce one after another. Because Wang refused to hand over the Chamber of Commerce, they withdrew at about 4 pm.

Losses of Japanese Ships in China After Economic Severance 111

▲ Japanese Ships Idle for 900,000 Tons in Three Months

▲ Business Losses of More Than 64 Million

Since the September 18th Incident, China has unanimously severed economic ties with Japan. The commercial losses suffered by Japan in China in these three months are greater than those of any previous boycott. The shipping companies have suffered the most. Whether it is the Yangtze River, inland rivers, ocean-going, or coastal shipping, Chinese merchants and passengers generally do not use Japanese ships, which can be said to be a complete break in trade. The losses of Japanese ships since the boycott have been detailedly investigated by reporters, and the accurate figures and their current operations are recorded as follows:

▲ Number of Ships Remaining on Route: This time, the severance of economic relations with Japan is carried out unanimously from top to bottom throughout the country, which is different from previous boycotts. In October, Japanese ships on all routes in the sea and river stopped service due to zero business. Up to now, only four ships remain on the upper and lower reaches of the Yangtze River. The 12 ships of the Kinai Shipping Company that specialize in Japan to Wuhu, Daye, Hankou, and other ports to transport steel and rapeseed have also stopped nine ships. The North and South Ocean routes along the coast, which used to have 70 to 80 Japanese ships, now have only 12 ships left. However, there is no cargo to transport and no passengers to carry. Most of them have to maintain their shipping rights because the Japanese government has subsidies. In terms of the situation, the Japanese ships in China today are only eking out a living.

▲ Losses of Various Shipping Companies: The Japan Shipowners' Association has investigated the operation of Japanese ships in China since September 18th. Counting to today, it has been exactly three months. During these three months, the three companies of Nisshin, Osaka, and Nittai Shipping, which have a large influence on the shipping industry in China, suffered the heaviest losses. From September 20th to December 14th, the three shipping companies suffered a total loss of 18,020,000 yen due to the impact of the economic severance. Due to the decline in the pound price, the companies lost another 8,640,000 yen, for a total loss of 26,660,000 yen.

▲ Losses of Ships Outside the Company: In addition to the above-mentioned three companies, there are also Kawasaki, Yamashita, Dalian, International, Mitsui, Sato, and Awa, Sawayama, Kyodo, Towa, and other Japanese companies that operate ships in China. The people of Shanghai call them "wild chicken ships," which usually travel to various ports in the North and South Oceans of our country. From September 20th to today, the business losses suffered by these ships outside the company due to the boycott and suspension of services are estimated at 37,800,000 yen.

▲ Surplus Tonnage: According to investigations by the Japan Shipowners' Association and the Seamen's Union, since the Manchurian Incident, due to the Chinese boycott of Japanese ships, the Japanese merchant ships that have been suspended in the first and second districts of the coastal routes (including the waterways in China, the North and South Oceans, the Yangtze River, and Korea) have reached 700,000 tons, and there is no way to dispatch them. The Pacific route in the ocean-going route has also been affected and 170,000 tons of ships have been idled. Due to the intense anti-Japanese sentiment of the overseas Chinese in the South Pacific Islands and Australia, 120,000 tons have also been suspended.

French Ambassador Denies Claims of French Troops Invading China 112

Shanghai Times reports: Regarding the rumors that Vietnamese French troops have invaded Guangxi, it is heard that the French ambassador to China, Mr. Wilden, received a telegram from the Vietnamese government last night, firmly denying the claim, saying that the French troops' actions were ordinary exercises.

Ma Xiangbo's Tearful Appeal to the Youth 113

The youth of the entire nation, alarmed by the rampant Japanese invaders, the collapse of justice, and the imminent peril of national demise, have spontaneously risen up to engage in the work of resisting Japan and saving the nation. Some have vowed to donate to General Ma Zhanshan, others have organized anti-Japanese support groups, still others have severed fingers or even resorted to suicide to awaken the people. Their courage is soaring and admirable. Upon hearing of this, this old man cannot help but feel admiration and respect, but I must sigh and say that today's affairs cannot be accomplished with mere passion. It is of little help to the nation. Saving the nation lies in practical struggle, especially in effective practical struggle. What is meant by effective practical struggle? The violent Japanese expose their imperialist ambitions, wielding their cannons and guns to forcibly occupy our land, slaughter our people, and seize our wealth. Their extreme greed can truly be described as the actions of robbers and communists. In essence, they can be regarded as international bandits. Why do I say this? Today's communism only shares wealth and goods, but Japan goes further by sharing people's land. Today's communists only share wealth and do not harm others' lives, but Japan not only forcibly occupies our land but also treats our men, women, old, and young as if they were mere grass, taking pleasure in slaughter. They spare no expense in staging extremely cruel tragedies everywhere with gunfire and cannons. This kind of banditry is exhibited by a nation and a country, so it is not inappropriate for us to call Japan an international bandit. Therefore, for our country to deal with this international bandit who is approaching step by step and entering our house, the question is not whether to fight or not, but how to fight and how to achieve effectiveness. This international bandit wields a strong army, navy, and air force to bully our weak country with its impoverished people and depleted resources. Although we have decided to resist, our military equipment and food supplies all depend on other countries. Resistance is not easy. In other words, rashly engaging in war is not a wise strategy. Therefore, how to struggle, how to make the struggle practical and effective, is truly the most urgent and serious problem that needs to be solved. Today, the only way for our country to save itself is not to seek help and pity from the League of Nations and the Kellogg-Briand Pact. However, from September 18th to today, more than eighty days have passed. What has been the result of seeking help and pity? The League of Nations is essentially the same as Japan, sharing the same odor and substance. Seeing the Japanese seize our Northeast, with its beautiful mountains and rivers and abundant resources, their index fingers have long been twitching, and they have long harbored plans to dip their fingers in the pot and take a share. Seeking skin from a tiger and asking for justice from the powerful is truly the greatest foolishness in the world. It is only enough to humiliate ourselves and invite disaster. Not seeking self-help but seeking help from others to侥幸establish a nation is a symbol of national demise and a truly heartbreaking phenomenon. Young people, what you are doing today is nothing more than petitioning in Nanjing or joining the army in the Northeast. Is this kind of work truly practical struggle? Is it truly effective practical struggle? Have you young people ever calmly considered this question? The country raises an army of more than two million, spending more than 80% of the national treasury. Since the founding of the Republic of China, wars have been frequent, and the tragedy of fratricide has been staged every day. However, when foreign aggression suddenly arrives, they retreat at the mere sight of the enemy. Within a day, half of the Northeast is lost to the enemy. At home, they only talk about鎮静 and sing about non-resistance. Abroad, they only beg and plead with the League of Nations, a puppet organization, presenting petitions and appeals, revealing their predicament. Students go to Beijing to petition, once, twice, and again, arriving and returning in an endless stream. Aside from hearing the usual "The central government is already prepared and has made a final resolution. The people should trust the government and support the government's teachings," the lost territory in the Northeast remains lost, the Japanese invaders remain rampant, and the internal divisions and conflicts remain the same. The government's inability to send troops, its lack of time to send troops, and its lack of resolve to send troops are obvious facts. The young people's arduous petitions and tearful pleas, even if they shed all their tears and then shed blood, and even if they die, are futile and of no benefit. Furthermore, General Ma Zhanshan, with his isolated army in a remote area, resists the strong and unyielding. Like strong wind revealing the strong grass, his righteousness is awe-inspiring. This responsible soldier is truly someone we should love, respect and support. However, our responsibility today is not only to save Ma Zhanshan but to save our entire country and our entire nation. Therefore, instead of merely admiring Ma Zhanshan, we should all rise up and strive to be like Ma Zhanshan, so that everyone is Ma Zhanshan. Moreover, along our coast and rivers, the violent Japanese warships are already densely deployed, and vagrant bandits are everywhere. They can fabricate pretexts and plant disasters to ignite the September 18th Incident at any time and place. Then, do we wait until it is lost before recovering it, or do we take advantage of the fact that it has not yet been occupied and properly preserve it? Therefore, today we should unite under the unified action of resisting violence and saving ourselves, and make preparations in advance. This old man believes that the most important strategy for saving the country today is to imitate the ancient system and implement the Baojia system. Ten families are united as one Jia, ten Jia as one Zhongjia, ten Zhongjia as one Dajia, ten Dajia as one Tuan, and ten Tuan as one Zhongguo, then Zhongguo becomes one Datuan. By expanding this, we can first create a population and household register, emulate the organization of the army, make actions unified, command swift, connections close, and will firm, lead it with non-cooperation with Japan, or economic severance with Japan, or even with a desperate battle with Japan. The Japanese criticize our national character, often calling it scattered sand. We should now use our greatest efforts to turn the scattered sand into strong cement. This old man says this, and I know that it is difficult to implement, but today the country is in danger and the situation is urgent, and we have no other choice. But if we use the spirit of going to Beijing to petition to engage in going to the countryside to awaken the masses, and use the determination of trekking long distances to the Northeast to support Ma Zhanshan to engage in organizing the masses, then gather the manpower and financial resources of hundreds of thousands of families, unite millions of people as one heart, and make them brave and knowledgeable, then what do we have to fear from the current national crisis, what do we have to fear from the invasion of the violent Japanese? Saving our country and renewing our nation all lie in this. This old man is old. Looking around at the mountains and rivers, I feel infinite emotion. I hate myself for being old and weak and unable to repay the country. Therefore, I have high hopes for my young students. This old man deeply believes that the country is based on the people. Without responsible citizens, the country will not be able to stand. At the same time, I deeply believe that self-help is the only way to save oneself. Only self-help can overcome the current difficulties. Seeking help from others and begging for pity from others are all futile. Youth is the backbone of society and the pillar of the country in the future. I hope you will work together with one heart and one mind to make arduous but effective struggles.
